- **16012**: Unity Concord is a system promulgated and managed by the Adventurers' Mutual Aid Network.
- **16013**: Participating adventurers are able to receive a variety of benefits and rewards just by engaging in their everyday activities.
- **16014**: "Unity" is a catchall term that refers to the group that participants belong to.
- **16015**: Unity leaders are individuals who have strong ties to adventurers' activities and are sterling representatives of their home nations.
- **16016**: Members of the same Unity can converse with each other over great distances through the use of specialized figurines known as "$5."
- **16017**: Chat settings may be changed by selecting "Status" from the main menu, and choosing "Unity Info" under the "Unity" submenu.
- **16018**: You may not always be able to join the chat if too many players are participating at once.
- **16019**: Those belonging to a Unity are able to undertake special Records of Eminence objectives related to Unity Concord activities.
- **16020**: The three pertinent categories include shared objectives, Unity leader-specific objectives, and Wanted battle objectives.
- **16021**: Shared objectives may be taken regardless of which Unity you have joined. These tasks can be undertaken at any time, and change every day at midnight (JST).
- **16022**: Unity leader-specific objectives are tied to the Unity's eponymous leader and change each week.
- **16023**: "Wanted" objectives center around vanquishing particularly heinous foes that terrorize Vana'diel.
- **16024**: These objectives are of a higher caliber, and thus require currency known as "Unity accolades" to undertake.
- **16025**: Shared and leader-specific objectives provide more accolades than run-of-the-mill objectives.
- **16026**: Vana'diel has always been plagued by nefarious foes pillaging the landscape, but relatives of some of the more heinous ones have been spotted lately.
- **16027**: The A.M.A.N. has deemed it necessary to eliminate these Wanted targets, and has notified Unity members that they are of the utmost priority.
- **16028**: A list of these foes can be viewed at any time by selecting the appropriate subcategory under the objectives list.
- **16029**: Unity Concord representatives are able to provide participants with transportation to the areas where these threats can be found.
- **16030**: Though tackling the profane will likely require participation of your allies, the objective can be undertaken so long as at least one person has set the appropriate objective.
- **16031**: When you set the objective and commence the battle, the requisite number of Unity accolades will be deducted from your total.
- **16032**: Successful challengers will be rewarded with special rewards in addition to the normal sparks of eminence.
- **16033**: No Unity accolades will be charged should you commence the battle without having the appropriate objective set, but the rewards you can reap from your efforts will be limited.
- **16034**: You can snatch unparalleled equipment and materials from the slain corpses of Wanted targets.
- **16035**: An A.M.A.N. specialist versed in arcane harmonization has kindly offered to use these materials to bring out the latent potential in such pieces.
- **16036**: One of the Unity guides will be pleased to accept certain combinations of equipment and materials to begin the process for you.
- **16037**: A number of accolades is required for this service, but the precision and accuracy of her methods are without equal, and there is no worry of your equipment being destroyed.
- **16038**: You can use specified materials to add new attributes to equipment that has been upgraded.
- **16039**: Utilizing additional materials after adding an attribute can accumulate Reinforcement Points for the equipment and increase its rank.
- **16040**: Increasing your equipment's rank can boost its attributes, while some equipment can also have additional attributes added later.
- **16041**: Speak to the Unity guides after gathering the necessary materials for your equipment in order to add attributes to it or increase its rank.
- **16042**: The first time you add an attribute to a piece of equipment will require the use of Unity accolades.
- **16043**: It also requires that you first complete a specific Records of Eminence objective.
- **16044**: The work you request will be carried out on-site by a specially trained Unity guide.
- **16045**: Completing Records of Eminence objectives as part of a Unity will reward you with Unity accolades in addition to sparks of eminence.
- **16046**: These accolades not only serve as a symbol of prestige, but can also be exchanged for a variety of services.
- **16047**: Some of these services include purchasing items, securing battle zones for hunting Wanted targets, fees for strengthening equipment, and more.
- **16048**: Please note that you may only exchange a maximum of $0 accolades per week (Earth time).
- **16049**: You may switch Unities once during the Unity ranking tabulation period.
- **16050**: This is not a decision to be taken lightly, for switching Unities will cause you to forfeit any benefits you were receiving from your previous one.
- **16051**: This process requires a fair deal of paperwork, and the A.M.A.N. will charge you an accolade fee based on your rank.
- **16052**: However, your valorous deeds remain wherever you choose to go, and you will not lose any other accolades.
- **16053**: Rankings are decided through the combined efforts of each of the Unity's members.
- **16054**: The A.M.A.N. tabulates all the good deeds done during a period of time and confers benefits on a Unity for the following ranking period.
- **16055**: Some of these benefits include changes to Unity accolades gained and the effects of equipment earned from Wanted battles.
- **16056**: Yes, you read that correctly--the attributes of certain equipment will increase in line with your Unity's ranking.
- **16057**: On the other hand, members of a Unity that finds itself on the lower rungs will enjoy an increase in accolades and capacity points earned to help bring them up to par.
